<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/><hr style='page-break-after:always;border:0;height:3pt;background-color:#909090;margin:8pt 0'/><p style='line-height:0;margin:0'></p>
<hr style='border:0;height:0;width:0;margin:14pt 0 0 0'/><table style='border-collapse:collapse;width:100%'><tr><td valign='top' style='width:10%'><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><b>Item 5.02.</b></p>
</td><td valign='top'><p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt'><b>Departure of Directors or Certain Officers; Election of Directors; Appointment of Certain Officers; Compensatory Arrangements of Certain Officers.</b></p>
</td></tr>

<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>In accordance with the Current Report on Form 8-K filed by Associated Banc-Corp (&#8220;Associated&#8221;) on March 10, 2021 (the &#8220;March 10 Form 8-K&#8221;), on April 28, 2021, Mr. Andrew J. Harmening assumed his position as President and Chief Executive Officer of Associated and joined Associated&#8217;s Board of Directors.&#160; Mr. Harmening also serves as President and Chief Executive Officer of Associated Bank, N.A. and President of Associated Trust,&#160;N.A. Mr. Harmening also chairs the Corporate Development Committee of the Board. Prior to joining Associated, Mr. Harmening, age 52, was the Senior Executive Vice President and Consumer and Business Banking Director at Huntington Bancshares from May 2017 to April 2021.&#160; Prior thereto, Mr. Harmening was with Bank of the West serving as vice chairman of the consumer banking division from July 2015 to May 2017, and as the senior executive vice president in the retail division from August 2007 to July 2015. &#160;&#160;He earned a bachelor&#8217;s degree from DePauw University and MBA from the University of Cincinnati.</p>
<p style='font:10pt Times New Roman;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:12pt;text-indent:36pt'>Mr. Harmening does not have any family relationships with any of Associated&#8217;s directors or executive officers and is not a party to any transactions listed in Item 404(a) of Regulation S-K. &#160;The description in the March&#160;10 Form 8-K of the letter agreement dated March 4, 2021 by and between Associated and Mr. Harmening setting forth the terms of Mr. Harmening&#8217;s employment with Associated and appointment to Associated&#8217;s Board of Directors is incorporated herein by reference.</p>
